#### Ask Anything

#### Ask AI Anything

Hi, I’m Trellis AI.  
I can answer any question you have about this case.  
You can ask me questions like:  
• "What is this case about in plain English?"  
• "Summarize the procedural history of this case."  
• "What motions have been filed and what were the outcomes?"  
• "Has the court ruled on class certification or summary judgment?"  
• "Who are the parties, attorneys, and judges involved?"  
• "Are there any upcoming deadlines or hearings?"  
• "Summarize arguments made by the defendant across all filings."

For full print and download access, please subscribe at https://www.trellis.law/.
